          function show_left_menu(showflag) {
            if (showflag == 1) {
              $(".hide-item").removeClass("hide-left-block");
              $(".hide-item").addClass("show-left-block");
            } else {
              $(".hide-item").addClass("hide-left-block");
              $(".hide-item").removeClass("show-left-block");
            }
          }

          $(document).ready(function() {
            var left_menu_cookie = "left-menu-hide";
            var left_menu_cookie_default = 1;
            if (/\-region/.test(window.location.href)) {
              left_menu_cookie = "left-menu-hide-regions";
              left_menu_cookie_default = 0;
            }

            $(".show-hide-left-block a").click(function() {
              var date = new Date();
              var minutes = 10;
              date.setTime(date.getTime() + (minutes * 60 * 1000));
              if (Cookies.get(left_menu_cookie) == 1) {
                Cookies.set(left_menu_cookie, 0, { expires: date });
                show_left_menu(0);
              }
              else {
                Cookies.set(left_menu_cookie, 1, { expires: date });
                show_left_menu(1);
              }
              return false;
            });

            if (! (typeof(Cookies.get(left_menu_cookie)) === "undefined")) {
              show_left_menu(Cookies.get(left_menu_cookie));
            }
            else {
              var date = new Date(); date.setTime(date.getTime() + (10 * 60 * 1000));
              Cookies.set(left_menu_cookie, left_menu_cookie_default, { expires: date });
              show_left_menu(left_menu_cookie_default);
            }
          });

function show_fields(el) {
  var vars = (el.value).split(':');
  var id = parseInt(vars[0]);
  var exists = 0 != $('#rooms option[value="к"]').length;
  var tables = [1, 1000, 2001];
  if(vars[1] == 'daily'){
    $("#rooms option[value='к']").remove();
  }
  else if(!exists && tables.indexOf(id) != -1){
    $("#rooms").prepend("<option value='к' selected>Комната</option>");
  }

  $.each($(el).prop('options'), function () {
      $('.object_type-' + parseInt(this.value)).hide();
  });

  $('.object_type-' + id).show();
}

$(document).ready(function() {
  $(".tabs-menu a").click(function(event) {
    event.preventDefault();
    $(this).parent().addClass("current");
    $(this).parent().siblings().removeClass("current");
    var tab = $(this).attr("href");
    $(".tab-content").not(tab).css("display", "none");
    $(tab).fadeIn();
  });

  $('.search-new-select-simple').select2({
    dropdownParent: $('#tabs-container'),
    dropdownAutoWidth : true,
    width: 'auto',
    minimumResultsForSearch: Infinity
  });

  $.getJSON("https://realt.by/typo3temp/uedb_menu/tx_uedbmenu_pi1.json", function( locations ) {
    $('.search-new-text-select').select2({
      placeholder: 'Поиск по региону',
      data: locations,
      allowClear: true,
      language: 'ru',
      dropdownParent: $('#tabs-container')
    });
  });

  /*
  $('.search-new-text-select').select2({
    placeholder: 'Поиск по региону',
    // data: search_locations,
    allowClear: true,
    language: 'ru',
    dropdownParent: $('#tabs-container')
  });
  */

  $("#form").submit(function(e){
      $("div:hidden").each(function(){
         $(this).remove();
      });
      return true;
  });
});
</script><!-- ADD-ADVERT --><!-- </div> <!-- main-menu --></div> <!-- header --><!-- INNER-CONTENT --><div class="inner-content"> <!-- INDEX-LEFT-CONTENT --><div class="index-left-content hide-item
